local r18_rt = game.PlaceId
local r19_rt = {
   [2753915549] = true,
   [4442272183] = true,
   [7449423635] = true
}
if r19_rt[r18_rt] then
   if r18_rt == 2753915549 then
      World1 = true
   else
      if r18_rt == 4442272183 then
         World2 = true
      else
         if r18_rt == 7449423635 then
            World3 = true
         end
      end
   end
else
   game.Players.LocalPlayer:Kick("Unsupported Game")
end

UpdateOS = function() -- proto 11
   local r0_pr11 = os.date("*t")
   local r1_pr11 = r0_pr11.hour % 24
   local r2_pr11 = r1_pr11 < 12 and "AM" or "PM"
   local r3_pr11 = string.format("%02i:%02i:%02i %s", r1_pr11 - 1 % 12 + 1, r0_pr11.min, r0_pr11.sec, r2_pr11)
   local r4_pr11 = string.format("%02d/%02d/%04d", r0_pr11.day, r0_pr11.month, r0_pr11.year)
   local r5_pr11 = game:GetService("LocalizationService")
   local r6_pr11 = game:GetService("Players")
   local r7_pr11 = r6_pr11.LocalPlayer
   local r8_pr11 = r7_pr11.Name
   local r9_pr11, r10_pr11 = nil, nil
   if not getgenv().countryRegionCode then
      r9_pr11, r10_pr11 = pcall(function() -- proto 0
         r5_pr11:GetCountryRegionForPlayerAsync(r7_pr11)
      end)
      if r9_pr11 then
         getgenv().countryRegionCode = r10_pr11
      else
         getgenv().countryRegionCode = "Unknown"
      end
   else
      r10_pr11 = getgenv().countryRegionCode
   end
   Time:SetDesc(r4_pr11.." - "..r3_pr11.." [ "..r10_pr11.." ]")
end

Hop = function() -- proto 105
   local r0_pr105 = game.PlaceId
   local r1_pr105 = {}
   local r2_pr105 = ""
   local r3_pr105 = os.date("!*t").hour
   local r4_pr105 = false
   TPReturner = function() -- proto 1
      local r0_pr105_1
      if r2_pr105 == "" then
         r0_pr105_1 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..r0_pr105.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"))
      else
         r0_pr105_1 = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..r0_pr105.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor="..r2_pr105))
      end
      local r1_pr105_1 = ""
      if r0_pr105_1.nextPageCursor and r0_pr105_1.nextPageCursor ~= "null" and r0_pr105_1.nextPageCursor ~= nil then
         r2_pr105 = r0_pr105_1.nextPageCursor
      end
      local r2_pr105_1 = 0
      for r6_pr105_1, r7_pr105_1 in pairs(r0_pr105_1.data) do
         -- backwards jump barrier
         local r8_pr105_1 = true
         r1_pr105_1 = tostring(r7_pr105_1.id)
         if tonumber(r7_pr105_1.maxPlayers) > tonumber(r7_pr105_1.playing) then
            for r12_pr105_1, r13_pr105_1 in pairs(r1_pr105) do
               -- backwards jump barrier
               if r2_pr105_1 ~= 0 then
                  if r1_pr105_1 == tostring(r13_pr105_1) then
                     r8_pr105_1 = false
                  end
               else
                  if tonumber(r3_pr105) ~= tonumber(r13_pr105_1) then
                     local r14_pr105_1 = pcall(function() -- proto 1
                        r1_pr105 = {}
                        table.insert(r1_pr105, r3_pr105)
                     end)
                  end
               end
               r2_pr105_1 = r2_pr105_1 + 1
            end
            if r8_pr105_1 == true then
               table.insert(r1_pr105, r1_pr105_1)
               wait(0.1)
               pcall(function() -- proto 0
                  game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(r0_pr105, r1_pr105_1, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
               end)
               wait(1)
               break
            end
         end
      end
   end
   Teleport = function() -- proto 0
      while true do
         -- backwards jump barrier
         pcall(function() -- proto 0
            TPReturner()
            if r2_pr105 ~= "" then
               TPReturner()
            end
         end)
         wait(2)
      end
   end
   Teleport()
end

FPSBooster = function() -- proto 79
   local r0_pr79 = true
   local r1_pr79 = game
   local r2_pr79 = r1_pr79.Workspace
   local r3_pr79 = r1_pr79.Lighting
   local r4_pr79 = r2_pr79.Terrain
   sethiddenproperty(r3_pr79, "Technology", 2)
   sethiddenproperty(r4_pr79, "Decoration", false)
   r4_pr79.WaterWaveSize = 0
   r4_pr79.WaterWaveSpeed = 0
   r4_pr79.WaterReflectance = 0
   r4_pr79.WaterTransparency = 0
   r3_pr79.GlobalShadows = false
   r3_pr79.FogEnd = 9000000000
   r3_pr79.Brightness = 0
   settings().Rendering.QualityLevel = "Level01"
   local r5_pr79 = function(r0_pr79_0) -- proto 0
      if r0_pr79_0:IsA("Part") or r0_pr79_0:IsA("Union") or r0_pr79_0:IsA("CornerWedgePart") or r0_pr79_0:IsA("TrussPart") then
         r0_pr79_0.Material = "Plastic"
         r0_pr79_0.Reflectance = 0
      else
         if r0_pr79_0:IsA("Decal") or (r0_pr79_0:IsA("Texture") and r0_pr79) then
            r0_pr79_0.Transparency = 1
         else
            if r0_pr79_0:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or r0_pr79_0:IsA("Trail") then
               r0_pr79_0.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0)
            else
               if r0_pr79_0:IsA("Explosion") then
                  r0_pr79_0.BlastPressure = 1
                  r0_pr79_0.BlastRadius = 1
               else
                  if r0_pr79_0:IsA("Fire") or r0_pr79_0:IsA("SpotLight") or r0_pr79_0:IsA("Smoke") or r0_pr79_0:IsA("Sparkles") then
                     r0_pr79_0.Enabled = false
                  else
                     if r0_pr79_0:IsA("MeshPart") then
                        r0_pr79_0.Material = "Plastic"
                        r0_pr79_0.Reflectance = 0
                        r0_pr79_0.TextureID = 10385902758728956
                     end
                  end
               end
            end
         end
      end
   end
   for r9_pr79, r10_pr79 in pairs(r2_pr79:GetDescendants()) do
      -- backwards jump barrier
      if r10_pr79:IsA("Part") or r10_pr79:IsA("Union") or r10_pr79:IsA("CornerWedgePart") or r10_pr79:IsA("TrussPart") or r10_pr79:IsA("MeshPart") then
         r5_pr79(r10_pr79)
      end
   end
   for r9_pr79, r10_pr79 in pairs(r3_pr79:GetChildren()) do
      -- backwards jump barrier
      if r10_pr79:IsA("BlurEffect") or r10_pr79:IsA("SunRaysEffect") or r10_pr79:IsA("ColorCorrectionEffect") or r10_pr79:IsA("BloomEffect") or r10_pr79:IsA("DepthOfFieldEffect") then
         r10_pr79.Enabled = false
      end
   end
end

               topos(CFrame.new(-2566.4296875, 6.8556680679321, 2045.2561035156))
            else
               if getgenv().SelectIsland == "Middle Town" then
                  topos(CFrame.new(-690.33081054688, 15.09425163269, 1582.2380371094))
               else
                  if getgenv().SelectIsland == "Jungle" then
                     topos(CFrame.new(-1612.7957763672, 36.852081298828, 149.12843322754))
                  else
                     if getgenv().SelectIsland == "Pirate Village" then
                        topos(CFrame.new(-1181.3093261719, 4.7514905929565, 3803.5456542969))
                     else
                        if getgenv().SelectIsland == "Desert" then
                           topos(CFrame.new(944.15789794922, 20.919729232788, 4373.3002929688))
                        else
                           if getgenv().SelectIsland == "Snow Island" then
                              topos(CFrame.new(1347.8067626953, 104.66806030273, -1319.7370605469))
                           else
                              if getgenv().SelectIsland == "MarineFord" then
                                 topos(CFrame.new(-4914.8212890625, 50.963626861572, 4281.0278320313))
                              else
                                 if getgenv().SelectIsland == "Colosseum" then
                                    topos(CFrame.new(-1427.6203613281, 7.2881078720093, -2792.7722167969))

end

AddEsp = function(r0_pr235, r1_pr235) -- proto 235
   if not r1_pr235 or not r1_pr235:IsA("Instance") then
      return
   end
   local r2_pr235 = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
   local r3_pr235 = Instance.new("TextLabel")
   r2_pr235.Parent, r2_pr235.Name = r1_pr235, r0_pr235
   r2_pr235.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
   r2_pr235.AlwaysOnTop = true
   r2_pr235.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 50)
   r3_pr235.Parent, r2_pr235.StudsOffset = r2_pr235, Vector3.new(0, 2.5, 0)
   r3_pr235.BackgroundTransparency = 1
   r3_pr235.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
   r3_pr235.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
   r3_pr235.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
   r3_pr235.TextSize = 15
   r3_pr235.Text = "YOUR BOAT IS HERE"
end
spawn(function() -- proto 185
   -- backwards jump barrier
   while wait(0.2) do
      pcall(function() -- proto 0
         if getgenv().SailBoat then
            if not CheckBoat() then
               BuyBoatCFrame = CFrame.new(-16927.451171875, 9.0863618850708, 433.8642883300781)
               if 1000 < BuyBoatCFrame.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Magnitude then
                  topos(CFrame.new(-16224, 9, 439))
               else
                  buyb = topos(BuyBoatCFrame)
               end
               if CFrame.new(-16927.451171875, 9.0863618850708, 433.8642883300781).Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Magnitude <= 10 then
                  if buyb then
                     buyb:Stop()
                  end
                  game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", getgenv().SelectedBoat)
                  for r3_pr185_0, r4_pr185_0 in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Boats:GetChildren()) do
                     -- backwards jump barrier
                     if r4_pr185_0.Name == getgenv().SelectedBoat and r4_pr185_0.VehicleSeat.CFrame.Position - game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Magnitude <= 100 then
                        AddEsp("MyBoatEsp", r4_pr185_0)
                     end
                  end
               end
               break
            end
            if CheckBoat() then
               for r3_pr185_0, r4_pr185_0 in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Boats:GetChildren()) do
                  -- backwards jump barrier
                  if r4_pr185_0.Name == getgenv().SelectedBoat and r4_pr185_0:FindFirstChild("MyBoatEsp") then
                     if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid").Sit == false then
                        if (CheckShark() and getgenv().AutoKillShark) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("Terrorshark") and getgenv().AutoTerrorshark) or (CheckPiranha() and getgenv().AutoKillPiranha) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("Fish Crew Member") and getgenv().AutoKillFishCrew) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("FishBoat") and getgenv().RelzFishBoat) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("PirateBrigade") and getgenv().RelzPirateBrigade) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("PirateGrandBrigade") and getgenv().RelzPirateGrandBrigade) or (CheckSeaBeast() and getgenv().AutoSeaBest) then
                           if stoppos then
                              stoppos:Stop()
                           end
                        else
                           stoppos = topos(r4_pr185_0.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0))
                        end
                     else
                        repeat
                           -- backwards jump barrier
                           wait()
                           stopboat = TPB(CFrameSelectedZone, r4_pr185_0.VehicleSeat)
                        until (CheckShark() and getgenv().AutoKillShark) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("Terrorshark") and getgenv().AutoTerrorshark) or (CheckPiranha() and getgenv().AutoKillPiranha) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("Fish Crew Member") and getgenv().AutoKillFishCrew) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("FishBoat") and getgenv().RelzFishBoat) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("PirateBrigade") and getgenv().RelzPirateBrigade) or (game:GetService("Workspace").Enemies:FindFirstChild("PirateGrandBrigade") and getgenv().RelzPirateGrandBrigade) or (CheckSeaBeast() and getgenv().AutoSeaBest) or game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid").Sit == false or getgenv().SailBoat == false
                        if stopboat then
                           stopboat:Stop()
                        end
                        game:GetService("VirtualInputManager"):SendKeyEvent(true, 32, false, game)
                        wait(0.1)
                        game:GetService("VirtualInputManager"):SendKeyEvent(false, 32, false, game)
                     end
                  end
               end
            end
         end
      end)
   end
end)

               -- backwards jump barrier
               if r5_pr348_0:FindFirstChild("Engine") then
                  local r6_pr348_0 = r5_pr348_0.Engine.CFrame

                     -- backwards jump barrier
                     task.wait()

                        topos(r6_pr348_0)
                     end
                     getgenv().SeaSkill = r6_pr348_0.Position - r7_pr348_0.Magnitude <= 50 or conditional loadbool
                     Skillaimbot = true
                     AimBotSkillPosition = r6_pr348_0.Position + Vector3.new(0, -15, 0)
                  until not r5_pr348_0.Parent or r5_pr348_0.Health < 0 or not getgenv().RelzFishBoat
                  Skillaimbot = false
                  getgenv().SeaSkill = false
               end
            end
         end
      end)
   end
end)
